CREATE TABLE SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
(
    GROU_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    NOTE VARCHAR2(100),
    NN NUMBER,
    SUM_TYPE VARCHAR2(100),
    DEALDATE VARCHAR2(8)
)
TABLESPACE DBACCADM_DATA_01;

CREATE TABLE SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
(
    TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    RUN_TIME DATE
)
TABLESPACE DBACCADM_DATA_01;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('市场部日报运行开始',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

CREATE TABLE SCB_D_S_CHECK_STB1 AS
SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE,'0' CHECK_SIGN FROM DUAL;

BEGIN
SCB_D_S_CK_PRE@O38;

END;
/

--数字新增主卡用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.USER_NO) NN,'100' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%集团%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                    UNION ALL
                    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%个人%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.USER_NO LIKE '%11'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
) TS
GROUP BY TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('数字新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--高清新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TC.GROUP_NAME,'' NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT D.ID_NO),'101' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D 
JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO T ON T.ID_NO=D.ID_NO
JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TC ON TC.CUST_ID=T.CUST_ID
WHERE D.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')=TRUNC(SYSDATE-1,'DD')
AND D.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%')
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D2 WHERE D2.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D2.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')<TRUNC(SYSDATE-1,'DD')
AND D2.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%') AND D2.ID_NO=D.ID_NO)
GROUP BY TC.GROUP_NAME;
COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('高清新增',SYSDATE);


COMMIT;

--互动新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'102' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('互动新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------宽带新增
--宽带新增用户
CREATE TABLE DAILY_KD_INCREASING1 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        UNION ALL
		                        SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
		                        FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
		                        LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
		                                LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
		                                        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
		                                                WHERE EXISTS (
		                                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
		                                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
		                                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
		                                                )
		                                                AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
		                                                AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
		                                                        AND EXISTS (
		                                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
		                                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
		                                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
		                                                        )
		                                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
		                                                AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
		                                                AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
		                                                UNION ALL
			                                                SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
			                                                FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
			                                                LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
			                                                        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
			                                                                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
			                                                                        WHERE EXISTS (
			                                                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
			                                                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G'))
			                                                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
			                                                                        )
			                                                                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
			                                                                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
			                                                                                AND EXISTS (
			                                                                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
			                                                                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G'))
			                                                                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
			                                                                                )
			                                                                                AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
			                                                                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
			                                                                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

--合作转自主
CREATE TABLE KD_HTOZ1 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        WHERE EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
        )
        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
        AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=TUI.CUST_ID
                    AND EXISTS (
                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                    )
                    AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                   )
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO TC2
            WHERE EXISTS (
                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP2
                WHERE TPP2.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                AND TPP2.OFFERID = TC2.OFFERID
            )
            AND TC2.CUSTID = T.CUSTID
        )
        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

----自主转合作
CREATE TABLE KD_ZTOH1 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        WHERE EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
        )
        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
        AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=TUI.CUST_ID
                    AND EXISTS (
                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                    )
                    AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                   )
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO TC2
            WHERE EXISTS (
                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP2
                WHERE TPP2.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                AND TPP2.OFFERID = TC2.OFFERID
            )
            AND TC2.CUSTID = T.CUSTID
        )
        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

--宽带同时订购无现金
CREATE TABLE KD_NOCASH1 AS
SELECT TUI.CUST_ID,TUI.ID_NO,B3.USER_CASH+B3.QT_SPECIAL_CASH+B3.CUST_SPECIAL_CASH CASH
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN BALANCES_INFO_03 B3 ON B3.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID AND B3.ID_NO = TUI.ID_NO
                WHERE EXISTS (
                    SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                    WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510) AND TP.VODMARK1 <> 'BTJ')
                    AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                )
                AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                AND TUI.CUST_ID IN (
                    SELECT TUI.CUST_ID
                    FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                    LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
                            WHERE EXISTS (
                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510) AND TP.VODMARK1 <> 'BTJ')
                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                            )
                            AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                            AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                            INTERSECT
                            SELECT TUI.CUST_ID
                            FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                            LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
                                    WHERE EXISTS (
                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                                    )
                                    AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                                    AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                )
                AND B3.USER_CASH+B3.QT_SPECIAL_CASH+B3.CUST_SPECIAL_CASH = 0;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.ID_NO) NN,'103' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM DAILY_KD_INCREASING1 T
WHERE T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ1)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_ZTOH1)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_NOCASH1)
GROUP BY T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('宽带新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'104' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

--新增高清38客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TCI.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.CUSTID) NN,'109' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERCOMPORDINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = T.CUSTID
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                WHERE T.OFFERCOMBID IN ('SC123891','SC123767')
                AND T.ORDERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND  TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                GROUP BY TCI.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('高清38新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--新增新全享客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TCI.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.CUSTID) NN,'105' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERCOMPORDINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = T.CUSTID
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                WHERE T.OFFERCOMBID IN ('SC123662','SC123663','SC123664','SC123650','SC123656','SC123657','SC123658','SC123659','SC123660','SC123645','SC123654','SC123661')
                AND T.ORDERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND  TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                GROUP BY TCI.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('新全享新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--新增老全享套餐客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TSS.OPERATION,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TSS.TERMINAL_NO) NN,'113' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT TS.GROUP_NAME2 OPERATION,TS.NOTE 客户所属经营部,TS.GROUP_ID 项目ID,TS.GROUP_NAME 项目名称,
    TS.ADDRESS_NAME 标准地址,TS.AD2 门牌号,TS.TERMINAL_NO,TS.CUST_NAME 客户名称,
    TS.CONTACT_PHONE 联系电话,TS.USER_NO,TS.IC_NO 智能卡号,TS.OFFERID 套餐ID,TS.OFFERNAME 套餐名称,
    TS.PROD_STATUS 套餐状态,TS.ORDERDATE 订购时间
    FROM (SELECT T.ORDERNO,T.OPTRID,T.OFFERID,T.ORDERDATE,TUI.IC_NO,
          (SELECT TP.OFFERNAME FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TP WHERE TP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID) OFFERNAME,
          (SELECT DA.USER_NO FROM DACCOUNTIDINFO DA WHERE DA.MSISDN = DG.PHONE_NO) USER_NO,
          (SELECT TPP.PRODSTATUSNAME FROM T_PP_PRODOFFERSTATUSCODE TPP WHERE TPP.PRODSTATUS = SUBSTR(T.PRODSTATUS,2,1)) PROD_STATUS,
          TG.TERMINAL_NO,DC.CUST_NAME,DC.CONTACT_PHONE,DCH.GROUP_ID,DCH.GROUP_NAME,DCHN.NOTE,DCHNAD.ADDRESS_NAME,DCHNA.ADDRESS_NAME AD2,
          (SELECT DI.GROUP_NAME FROM DCHNGROUPMSG DI WHERE DI.GROUP_ID=DC.GROUP_ID) GROUP_NAME2
          FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
          JOIN DCUSTMSG DG ON DG.ID_NO=TO_NUMBER(T.USERID)
                                       JOIN DCUSTDOC DC ON DC.CUST_ID=T.CUSTID
                                               JOIN DCUSTTERMINALMSG TG ON TG.CUST_ID = DC.CUST_ID
                                                       JOIN DANALOGMSGADD DANA ON DANA.TERMINAL_NO = TG.TERMINAL_NO
                                                               JOIN DCHNADDRESSDETAILMSG DCHNA ON DCHNA.ADDRESS_ID = DANA.ADDR_ID
                                                                       LEFT JOIN DCHNPROJECTMSG DCHN ON DCHN.TEMP1 = DCHNA.PARENT_ADDRESS_ID
                                                                               LEFT JOIN DCHNGROUPMSG DCH ON DCH.GROUP_ID = DCHN.GROUP_ID
                                                                                       LEFT JOIN DCHNADDRESSMSGSC DCHNAD ON DCHNAD.ADDRESS_ID = DCHNA.PARENT_ADDRESS_ID
                                                                                               LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = DG.ID_NO
                                                                                                       WHERE T.OFFERID = 'SC122924'
         ) TS
    WHERE TS.ORDERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
) TSS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.TERMINAL_NO = TSS.TERMINAL_NO
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                GROUP BY TSS.OPERATION,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('老全享新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--自有高清新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TC.GROUP_NAME,'' NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT D.ID_NO),'110' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D 
JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO T ON T.ID_NO=D.ID_NO
JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TC ON TC.CUST_ID=T.CUST_ID
WHERE D.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')=TRUNC(SYSDATE-1,'DD')--时间条件
AND D.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB 'AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%')--换上的机顶盒为H
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D2 WHERE D2.UPDATE_TYPE='A' --排除历史机顶盒为H
    AND TRUNC(D2.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')<TRUNC(SYSDATE-1,'DD')
    AND D2.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S 
    WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB 'AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%') AND D2.ID_NO=D.ID_NO)
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T4--排除当前订购爱家套餐
    WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP4
    WHERE TPP4.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP4.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP4 WHERE TP4.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
    AND TPP4.OFFERID = T4.OFFERID) AND TO_NUMBER(T4.USERID)=T.ID_NO)
GROUP BY TC.GROUP_NAME;
COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('-7.自有高清新增',SYSDATE);
COMMIT;

--自有互动新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'111' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND T.USERID NOT IN (
                            SELECT T.USERID FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                            WHERE EXISTS (
                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                            )
                        )
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('-6.自有互动新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--自有宽带新增用户

SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.ID_NO) NN,'112' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM DAILY_KD_INCREASING1 T
WHERE T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ1)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ1)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_NOCASH1)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (
    SELECT T.USERID FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
    WHERE EXISTS (
        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
    )
)
GROUP BY T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE;

COMMIT;

--存500送500新增客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.客户号) NN,'116' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT D.LOGIN_ACCEPT 流水号,D.ACTIVITY_ID 营销活动ID,(SELECT MA.ACTIVITY_NAME FROM MK_ACTRULE_DICT MA WHERE MA.ACTIVITY_ID = D.ACTIVITY_ID) 营销活动名称,D.CUST_ID,TCI.TERMINAL_NO 客户号,
    TCI.CUST_NAME,TCI.GROUP_NAME,D.CONTRACT_NO 账本号,D.TOTAL_FEE 金额,
    D.LOGIN_NO 操作员,D.OP_CODE 操作代码,(SELECT TRIM(S.FUNCTION_NAME) FROM SFUNCCODE S WHERE S.FUNCTION_CODE = D.OP_CODE) FUNCTION_NAME,D.OP_TIME 操作时间,
    D.END_TIME 活动结束时间,D.OP_NOTE
    FROM MK_ACT_INFO D
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = D.CUST_ID
            WHERE D.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
            AND D.ACTIVITY_ID IN ('A0000312')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.TERMINAL_NO = TS.客户号
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                WHERE TS.GROUP_NAME IS NOT NULL
                GROUP BY TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('-3.存500送500新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

    TCI.CUST_NAME,TCI.GROUP_NAME,D.CONTRACT_NO 账本号,D.TOTAL_FEE 金额,
    D.LOGIN_NO 操作员,D.OP_CODE 操作代码,(SELECT TRIM(S.FUNCTION_NAME) FROM SFUNCCODE S WHERE S.FUNCTION_CODE = D.OP_CODE) FUNCTION_NAME,D.OP_TIME 操作时间,
    D.END_TIME 活动结束时间,D.OP_NOTE

--赠送新增笔数
CREATE TABLE SCB_N9991
(
    GROU_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    NOTE VARCHAR2(100),
    LOGIN_ACCEPT VARCHAR2(100),
    CASH_PAY VARCHAR2(100),
    SUM_TYPE VARCHAR2(100),
    DEALDATE VARCHAR2(8)
);

DECLARE
YESTERDAY_B VARCHAR2(30);

YESTERDAY_E VARCHAR2(30);

YESTERDAY VARCHAR2(30);

MONTHNOW VARCHAR2(6);

MONTHBEF VARCHAR2(6);

BEGIN
SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00' INTO YESTERDAY_B FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59' INTO YESTERDAY_E FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYYMMDD') INTO YESTERDAY  FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE,0),'YYYYMM') INTO MONTHNOW FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE,-1),'YYYYMM') INTO MONTHBEF FROM DUAL;

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9991
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''118'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A915'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9991
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''119'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A916'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9991
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''120'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A917'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

END;

/
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS1
SELECT TSS.GROU_NAME,TSS.NOTE,TSS.NN,TSS.SUM_TYPE,TSS.DEALDATE FROM (
    SELECT TS.DEALDATE,TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,TS.SUM_TYPE,SUM(COUNT_NUM) NN FROM (
        SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,T.SUM_TYPE,T.LOGIN_ACCEPT,(CASE WHEN T.CASH_PAY > 0 THEN 1 WHEN T.CASH_PAY < 0 THEN -1 END) COUNT_NUM,T.CASH_PAY,T.DEALDATE
        FROM SCB_N9991 T
    ) TS
    GROUP BY TS.DEALDATE,TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,TS.SUM_TYPE
) TSS;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS1
VALUES ('-1.电视机销售新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

                WHERE T.OFFERCOMBID IN ('SC124621')
                AND T.ORDERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND  TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-1,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                GROUP BY TCI.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

--数字新增主卡用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.USER_NO) NN,'100' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%集团%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                    UNION ALL
                    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%个人%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.USER_NO LIKE '%11'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
) TS
GROUP BY TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('数字新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--高清新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TC.GROUP_NAME,'' NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT D.ID_NO),'101' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D 
JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO T ON T.ID_NO=D.ID_NO
JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TC ON TC.CUST_ID=T.CUST_ID
WHERE D.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')=TRUNC(SYSDATE-2,'DD')
AND D.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%')
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D2 WHERE D2.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D2.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')<TRUNC(SYSDATE-2,'DD')
AND D2.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%') AND D2.ID_NO=D.ID_NO)
GROUP BY TC.GROUP_NAME;
COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('高清新增',SYSDATE);


COMMIT;

--互动新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'102' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

--宽带新增用户
CREATE TABLE DAILY_KD_INCREASING2 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        UNION ALL
		                        SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
		                        FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
		                        LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
		                                LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
		                                        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
		                                                WHERE EXISTS (
		                                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
		                                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
		                                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
		                                                )
		                                                AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
		                                                AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
		                                                        AND EXISTS (
		                                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
		                                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168'))
		                                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
		                                                        )
		                                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
		                                                AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
		                                                AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
		                                                UNION ALL
			                                                SELECT TUI.ID_NO,TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE
			                                                FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
			                                                LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
			                                                        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
			                                                                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
			                                                                        WHERE EXISTS (
			                                                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
			                                                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G'))
			                                                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
			                                                                        )
			                                                                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
			                                                                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
			                                                                                AND EXISTS (
			                                                                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
			                                                                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G'))
			                                                                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
			                                                                                )
			                                                                                AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
			                                                                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
			                                                                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

--合作转自主
CREATE TABLE KD_HTOZ2 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        WHERE EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
        )
        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
        AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=TUI.CUST_ID
                    AND EXISTS (
                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                    )
                    AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                   )
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO TC2
            WHERE EXISTS (
                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP2
                WHERE TPP2.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                AND TPP2.OFFERID = TC2.OFFERID
            )
            AND TC2.CUSTID = T.CUSTID
        )
        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

----自主转合作
CREATE TABLE KD_ZTOH2 AS
SELECT TUI.ID_NO
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        WHERE EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
        )
        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
        AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=TUI.CUST_ID
                    AND EXISTS (
                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                        AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                    )
                    AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                   )
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT * FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO TC2
            WHERE EXISTS (
                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP2
                WHERE TPP2.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510))
                AND TPP2.OFFERID = TC2.OFFERID
            )
            AND TC2.CUSTID = T.CUSTID
        )
        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2);

--宽带同时订购无现金
CREATE TABLE KD_NOCASH2 AS
SELECT TUI.CUST_ID,TUI.ID_NO,B3.USER_CASH+B3.QT_SPECIAL_CASH+B3.CUST_SPECIAL_CASH CASH
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN BALANCES_INFO_03 B3 ON B3.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID AND B3.ID_NO = TUI.ID_NO
                WHERE EXISTS (
                    SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                    WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510) AND TP.VODMARK1 <> 'BTJ')
                    AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                )
                AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                AND TUI.CUST_ID IN (
                    SELECT TUI.CUST_ID
                    FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                    LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
                            WHERE EXISTS (
                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10509,10510) AND TP.VODMARK1 <> 'BTJ')
                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                            )
                            AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                            AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                            INTERSECT
                            SELECT TUI.CUST_ID
                            FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                            LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
                                    WHERE EXISTS (
                                        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('G','168','H168'))
                                        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                                    )
                                    AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                                    AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                )
                AND B3.USER_CASH+B3.QT_SPECIAL_CASH+B3.CUST_SPECIAL_CASH = 0;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.ID_NO) NN,'103' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM DAILY_KD_INCREASING2 T
WHERE T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ2)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_ZTOH2)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_NOCASH2)
GROUP BY T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('宽带新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID

                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID

                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID

                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)

--新增老全享套餐客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TSS.OPERATION,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TSS.TERMINAL_NO) NN,'113' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT TS.GROUP_NAME2 OPERATION,TS.NOTE 客户所属经营部,TS.GROUP_ID 项目ID,TS.GROUP_NAME 项目名称,
    TS.ADDRESS_NAME 标准地址,TS.AD2 门牌号,TS.TERMINAL_NO,TS.CUST_NAME 客户名称,
    TS.CONTACT_PHONE 联系电话,TS.USER_NO,TS.IC_NO 智能卡号,TS.OFFERID 套餐ID,TS.OFFERNAME 套餐名称,
    TS.PROD_STATUS 套餐状态,TS.ORDERDATE 订购时间
    FROM (SELECT T.ORDERNO,T.OPTRID,T.OFFERID,T.ORDERDATE,TUI.IC_NO,
          (SELECT TP.OFFERNAME FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TP WHERE TP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID) OFFERNAME,
          (SELECT DA.USER_NO FROM DACCOUNTIDINFO DA WHERE DA.MSISDN = DG.PHONE_NO) USER_NO,
          (SELECT TPP.PRODSTATUSNAME FROM T_PP_PRODOFFERSTATUSCODE TPP WHERE TPP.PRODSTATUS = SUBSTR(T.PRODSTATUS,2,1)) PROD_STATUS,
          TG.TERMINAL_NO,DC.CUST_NAME,DC.CONTACT_PHONE,DCH.GROUP_ID,DCH.GROUP_NAME,DCHN.NOTE,DCHNAD.ADDRESS_NAME,DCHNA.ADDRESS_NAME AD2,
          (SELECT DI.GROUP_NAME FROM DCHNGROUPMSG DI WHERE DI.GROUP_ID=DC.GROUP_ID) GROUP_NAME2
          FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
          JOIN DCUSTMSG DG ON DG.ID_NO=TO_NUMBER(T.USERID)
                                       JOIN DCUSTDOC DC ON DC.CUST_ID=T.CUSTID
                                               JOIN DCUSTTERMINALMSG TG ON TG.CUST_ID = DC.CUST_ID
                                                       JOIN DANALOGMSGADD DANA ON DANA.TERMINAL_NO = TG.TERMINAL_NO
                                                               JOIN DCHNADDRESSDETAILMSG DCHNA ON DCHNA.ADDRESS_ID = DANA.ADDR_ID
                                                                       LEFT JOIN DCHNPROJECTMSG DCHN ON DCHN.TEMP1 = DCHNA.PARENT_ADDRESS_ID
                                                                               LEFT JOIN DCHNGROUPMSG DCH ON DCH.GROUP_ID = DCHN.GROUP_ID
                                                                                       LEFT JOIN DCHNADDRESSMSGSC DCHNAD ON DCHNAD.ADDRESS_ID = DCHNA.PARENT_ADDRESS_ID
                                                                                               LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = DG.ID_NO
                                                                                                       WHERE T.OFFERID = 'SC122924'
         ) TS
    WHERE TS.ORDERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
) TSS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.TERMINAL_NO = TSS.TERMINAL_NO
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                GROUP BY TSS.OPERATION,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('老全享新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--自有高清新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TC.GROUP_NAME,'' NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT D.ID_NO),'110' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D 
JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO T ON T.ID_NO=D.ID_NO
JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TC ON TC.CUST_ID=T.CUST_ID
WHERE D.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')=TRUNC(SYSDATE-2,'DD')--时间条件
AND D.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB 'AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%')--换上的机顶盒为H
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D2 WHERE D2.UPDATE_TYPE='A' --排除历史机顶盒为H
    AND TRUNC(D2.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')<TRUNC(SYSDATE-2,'DD')
    AND D2.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S 
    WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB 'AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%') AND D2.ID_NO=D.ID_NO)
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T4--排除当前订购爱家套餐
    WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP4
    WHERE TPP4.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP4.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP4 WHERE TP4.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
    AND TPP4.OFFERID = T4.OFFERID) AND TO_NUMBER(T4.USERID)=T.ID_NO)
GROUP BY TC.GROUP_NAME;
COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('-7.自有高清新增',SYSDATE);
COMMIT;

--自有互动新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'111' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND T.USERID NOT IN (
                            SELECT T.USERID FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
                            WHERE EXISTS (
                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
                                AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                            )
                        )
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('-6.自有互动新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT T.ID_NO) NN,'112' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM DAILY_KD_INCREASING2 T
WHERE T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ2)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_HTOZ2)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (SELECT ID_NO FROM KD_NOCASH2)
AND T.ID_NO NOT IN (
    SELECT T.USERID FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
    WHERE EXISTS (
        SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
        WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODMARK1 IN ('168','H168','G'))
        AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
    )
)
GROUP BY T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE;

COMMIT;

--存500送500新增客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.客户号) NN,'116' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT D.LOGIN_ACCEPT 流水号,D.ACTIVITY_ID 营销活动ID,(SELECT MA.ACTIVITY_NAME FROM MK_ACTRULE_DICT MA WHERE MA.ACTIVITY_ID = D.ACTIVITY_ID) 营销活动名称,D.CUST_ID,TCI.TERMINAL_NO 客户号,
    TCI.CUST_NAME,TCI.GROUP_NAME,D.CONTRACT_NO 账本号,D.TOTAL_FEE 金额,
    D.LOGIN_NO 操作员,D.OP_CODE 操作代码,(SELECT TRIM(S.FUNCTION_NAME) FROM SFUNCCODE S WHERE S.FUNCTION_CODE = D.OP_CODE) FUNCTION_NAME,D.OP_TIME 操作时间,
    D.END_TIME 活动结束时间,D.OP_NOTE
    FROM MK_ACT_INFO D
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = D.CUST_ID
            WHERE D.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
            AND D.ACTIVITY_ID IN ('A0000312')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.TERMINAL_NO = TS.客户号
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                WHERE TS.GROUP_NAME IS NOT NULL
                GROUP BY TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('-3.存500送500新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--存500送200新增客户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.客户号) NN,'117' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT D.LOGIN_ACCEPT 流水号,D.ACTIVITY_ID 营销活动ID,(SELECT MA.ACTIVITY_NAME FROM MK_ACTRULE_DICT MA WHERE MA.ACTIVITY_ID = D.ACTIVITY_ID) 营销活动名称,D.CUST_ID,TCI.TERMINAL_NO 客户号,
    TCI.CUST_NAME,TCI.GROUP_NAME,D.CONTRACT_NO 账本号,D.TOTAL_FEE 金额,
    D.LOGIN_NO 操作员,D.OP_CODE 操作代码,(SELECT TRIM(S.FUNCTION_NAME) FROM SFUNCCODE S WHERE S.FUNCTION_CODE = D.OP_CODE) FUNCTION_NAME,D.OP_TIME 操作时间,
    D.END_TIME 活动结束时间,D.OP_NOTE
    FROM MK_ACT_INFO D
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = D.CUST_ID
            WHERE D.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
            AND D.ACTIVITY_ID IN ('A0000307')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.TERMINAL_NO = TS.客户号
        LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                WHERE TS.GROUP_NAME IS NOT NULL
                GROUP BY TS.GROUP_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('-2.存500送200新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--赠送新增笔数
CREATE TABLE SCB_N9992
(
    GROU_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    NOTE VARCHAR2(100),
    LOGIN_ACCEPT VARCHAR2(100),
    CASH_PAY VARCHAR2(100),
    SUM_TYPE VARCHAR2(100),
    DEALDATE VARCHAR2(8)
);

DECLARE
YESTERDAY_B VARCHAR2(30);

YESTERDAY_E VARCHAR2(30);

YESTERDAY VARCHAR2(30);

MONTHNOW VARCHAR2(6);

MONTHBEF VARCHAR2(6);

BEGIN
SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00' INTO YESTERDAY_B FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59' INTO YESTERDAY_E FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-2,'YYYYMMDD') INTO YESTERDAY  FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE,0),'YYYYMM') INTO MONTHNOW FROM DUAL;

SELECT TO_CHAR(ADD_MONTHS(SYSDATE,-1),'YYYYMM') INTO MONTHBEF FROM DUAL;

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9992
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''118'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A915'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9992
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''119'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A916'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
INSERT INTO SCB_N9992
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TS.LOGIN_ACCEPT,TS.CASH_PAY,''120'' SUM_TYPE,'||YESTERDAY||' DEALDATE
FROM (
SELECT  TUI.USER_NO,WG.TOTAL_DATE,WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT,WG.LOGIN_NO,WG.OP_CODE,WG.OP_TIME,
(SELECT WC2.FEE_CODE FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC2 WHERE WC2.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_CODE,
(SELECT (SELECT SS.OP_NOTE FROM SOPFEE SS WHERE SS.FEE_CODE = WC.FEE_CODE) FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) WC WHERE WC.LOGIN_ACCEPT = WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT) FEE_NAME,
WG.CASH_PAY,WG.SYSTEM_NOTE,WG.OP_NOTE,TUI.GROU_NAME
FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHG'||MONTHBEF||'
) WG
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = WG.ID_NO
WHERE WG.LOGIN_ACCEPT IN (SELECT W.LOGIN_ACCEPT FROM (
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHNOW||'
UNION ALL
SELECT * FROM WCHGDET'||MONTHBEF||'
) W WHERE W.OP_CODE= ''2202'' AND W.FEE_CODE = ''A917'')
AND WG.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
AND WG.OP_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_B||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'') AND TO_DATE('''||YESTERDAY_E||''',''YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'')
) TS
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.USER_NO = TS.USER_NO
LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
';

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
COMMIT
';

END;

/
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS2
SELECT TSS.GROU_NAME,TSS.NOTE,TSS.NN,TSS.SUM_TYPE,TSS.DEALDATE FROM (
    SELECT TS.DEALDATE,TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,TS.SUM_TYPE,SUM(COUNT_NUM) NN FROM (
        SELECT T.GROU_NAME,T.NOTE,T.SUM_TYPE,T.LOGIN_ACCEPT,(CASE WHEN T.CASH_PAY > 0 THEN 1 WHEN T.CASH_PAY < 0 THEN -1 END) COUNT_NUM,T.CASH_PAY,T.DEALDATE
        FROM SCB_N9992 T
    ) TS
    GROUP BY TS.DEALDATE,TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,TS.SUM_TYPE
) TSS;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS2
VALUES ('-1.电视机销售新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

(
    GROU_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    NOTE VARCHAR2(100),
    NN NUMBER,
    SUM_TYPE VARCHAR2(100),
    DEALDATE VARCHAR2(8)
)
TABLESPACE DBACCADM_DATA_01;

CREATE TABLE SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS3
(
    TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100),
    RUN_TIME DATE
)
TABLESPACE DBACCADM_DATA_01;

VALUES ('市场部日报运行开始',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--数字新增主卡用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS3
SELECT TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TS.USER_NO) NN,'100' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM (
    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%集团%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                    UNION ALL
                    SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,TUI.USER_NO
    FROM TEMP_USER_INFO TUI
    LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
            LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                    WHERE TCI.C_TYPE LIKE '%个人%'
                    AND TUI.HOSTMARK LIKE '%主卡%'
                    AND TUI.USER_NO LIKE '%11'
                    AND TUI.OPEN_TIME BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
) TS
GROUP BY TS.GROU_NAME,TS.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS3
VALUES ('数字新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;

--高清新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS3
SELECT TC.GROUP_NAME,'' NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT D.ID_NO),'101' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D 
JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO T ON T.ID_NO=D.ID_NO
JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TC ON TC.CUST_ID=T.CUST_ID
WHERE D.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')=TRUNC(SYSDATE-3,'DD')
AND D.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%')
AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM DUSERRESMSGHIS D2 WHERE D2.UPDATE_TYPE='A' AND TRUNC(D2.UPDATE_TIME,'DD')<TRUNC(SYSDATE-3,'DD')
AND D2.RES_TYPE IN (SELECT S.RES_TYPE FROM SRESTYPE S WHERE S.RES_CLASS='STB '
AND S.RES_NAME LIKE '%[%H%]%') AND D2.ID_NO=D.ID_NO)
GROUP BY TC.GROUP_NAME;
COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS3
VALUES ('高清新增',SYSDATE);


COMMIT;

--互动新增用户
INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_STATISTICS3
SELECT TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE,COUNT(DISTINCT TUI.ID_NO) NN,'102' SUM_TYPE,TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYYMMDD') DEALDATE
FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFO T
LEFT JOIN TEMP_USER_INFO TUI ON TUI.ID_NO = T.USERID
        LEFT JOIN TEMP_CUST_INFO_01 TCI ON TCI.CUST_ID = TUI.CUST_ID
                LEFT JOIN OBJECT_INFO_02 O ON O.OBJECT_CODE = TCI.OBJECT_CODE
                        WHERE EXISTS (
                            SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                            WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                            AND TPP.OFFERID = T.OFFERID
                        )
                        AND T.OPTDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS') AND TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 23:59:59','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS')
                        AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM T_CI_USERORDERINFOHIS TI WHERE TI.USERID=T.USERID
                                        AND EXISTS (
                                                SELECT * FROM T_PP_PRODOFFER TPP
                                                WHERE TPP.OFFERNAME IN (SELECT TP.PRODUCTNAME FROM TEMP_PRODUCTTYPE TP WHERE TP.VODCODE IN (10504,10505))
                                                AND TPP.OFFERID = TI.OFFERID
                                        )
                                        AND TI.OPTDATE < TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE-3,'YYYY-MM-DD')||' 00:00:00','YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS'))
                        AND T.PRODPRCID<>'Z0'
                        AND TUI.GROUP_ID IN (SELECT DI.GROUP_ID FROM DCHNGROUPINFO DI WHERE DI.PARENT_GROUP_ID=101 AND DI.PARENT_LEVEL=2)
                        GROUP BY TUI.GROU_NAME,O.NOTE;

COMMIT;

INSERT INTO SCB_DAILY_PROGRESS_STATUS3
VALUES ('互动新增',SYSDATE);

COMMIT;
